TRIAL WINNING DECKLISTS
=======================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX SALT LAKE CITY 2014 - COVERAGE - EVENTS](/en/events/coverage/gpslc14) 
 on September 6, 2014 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast











There are always perks to getting to the Grand Prix site early. Sure, you can peruse the dealers' tables or meet up with friends for a few drafts. But instead, infinitely more productive for the next morning, you could win a Grand Prix Trial (“Grinder”) the night before and net yourself precious byes for the coming tournament. There are worse feelings than waking up 2-0 on the first day, especially if you weren't expecting to.


Here are the decklists of the people lucky enough, and skilled enough, to have earned that glorious Saturday-morning wake-up feeling.







#### Jack Shart, Grand Prix Trial Winner


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-a3105b7fbf12fdacbd397d6f112c28f4?n=Jack%20Shart%2C%20Grand%20Prix%20Trial%20Winner)
